 He said, the ABCDE rule can be used to catch signs of melanoma: asymmetry or asymmetry - mole or one part of the birthmark not matching the other, border or border - irregular edges, color or complexion - of the entire skin
 The color does not remain the same, there may be brown, black, pink, red, white or blue spots elsewhere, diammeter or diameter - more than a quarter of an inch, evolving or developing
 There is a change in the shape, texture or color of the body

 — Narendra Modi (@narendramodi) 23 may 2017 Prime Minister Narendra Modi has expressed deep sorrow over the Manchester incident
 unhone twit karte hue is haadase main hataahat pariwaron ke prati gahari samvednaa prakat kii
 At the same time, @manchesterarena issued a statement that we confirm that an incident occurred here while returning from the Ariana Grand Show last night
 ye ghatana manchester erina ke baahar saarvajanik jagah par hui
 Our prayers and condolences are with the victim
 zyada apadet ke liye twitor par @gmpolice ko follow karen
 Pained by the attack in Manchester
 We strongly condemn it
 Our thoughts are with the families of the deceased & prayers with the injured

 The incident occurred in a public place outside the Manchester Arena
 hamaari prarthana or samvednaa peedit ke saath he

 nae saal (2016) ke liye apane arthshaastriyon dwaara pesh bhavishyavaanee prastut karte hue vaishvik paraamarsh company peedblusi ne kaha ki ubhartee arthvyavasthaaon main se sirf bharat ke 2016 ke dauraan dirghakaalik ausat vruddhi dar ke mukaable tej vruddhi darj karne kii ummid he
 The comments saat ubhartee arthvyavasthaaon - china, bharat, brazil, mexico, rus, indonesia tathaa turki - main se bharat kaa pradarshan sabase acha rahegaa, jabaki brazil or rus kii arthvyavastha main sankuchan tathaa china kii arthvyavastha main narmi aegi
 pwc said, 'we expect India to register faster growth than China for the second consecutive year and the actual growth is around 7
 7 pratishat rahegi
 'this year the G7 economies (US, Japan, Germany, UK, France, Italy and Canada) are now expected to register the fastest growth since 2010 for the first time
 iske ulat saat ubhartee arthvyavasthaaen apane rujhaan ke mukaable dhimi vruddhi darj karengi, lekin ji-7 ke mukaable phir bhi tej rahengi

 tippaniyan Out of the seven emerging economies - China, India, Brazil, Mexico, Russia, Indonesia and Turkey - India will be the best performer, while the economy of Brazil and Russia will slow down and China's economy will slow down

 bharat ke pehle khaas raksha upgrah jisat-7 ko aaj french guyana ke koru prakshepan sthal se safaltaapurvak prakshepit kar diya gaya
 It was launched through the Ariane-5 rocket of the European Space Agency Ariane Space
 isse desh ko samudri suraksha ke kshetra main kaaphi majbootee milegi
 The Indian Navy will use this multi-band communication satellite manufactured in the country, which is expected to start operations by the end of September
 jisat-7 upgrah par 185 karod rupee kii laagat ai he
 It is the first satellite in the country, dedicated to the defense sector
 upgrah ke prakshepan kii prakriya tadake 2 baje shuru hui, jo 50 minute tak chali
 After a flight of about 34 minutes, it was sent to the 'geosynchronous Transfer Orbit' of 249 km 'periji' (earth's closest point in orbit) and 35,929 km 'apoji' (earth's farthest point in orbit)
 31 agast se 4 sitambar tak bhartiya antariksh anusandhan sanghathan (isro) upgrah ko bumadhya rekha ke 36,000 kilometre upar ‘jeeosteshnari orbit' main pahunchane ke liye ise kaksha main upar uthaane ke liye teen abhiyaan chalaaegaa
 By September 14, the satellite will be placed in its orbit 74 degrees east longitude and then its transponders will be operational
 jisat-7 ke frequency band antariksh aadhaarit samudri sanchaar main madad karenge

 tippaniyan According to a senior space scientist, as far as space-based communication is concerned, the Navy has had many limitations till now

 Earlier, satellite communication in ships was done through global mobile satellite communication service provider 'INMARSAT'
 atyaadhunik upgrah main uchaef, es, si or kyuu bainds main sanchalit hone vaale upkaran lage hai
 It had a launch weight of 2625 kg and is based on isro's 2500 kg satellite bus with some new technologies including Antina
 isro ko beemaa sahit iske prakshepan par 470 karod rupee kaa kharch vahan karnaa padaa he
 This will give the country considerable strength in the field of maritime security
 bhartiya nausena desh main nirmit is multi-band sanchaar upgrah kaa istemaal karegi, jiskaa sitambar ke ant tak parichaalan shuru ho jane kii ummid he

 yah desh kaa pehla upgrah he, jo raksha kshetra ke liye samarpit he
 The satellite launch process started at 2 am, which lasted for 50 minutes
 kareeb 34 minute kii udaan ke baad ise 249 kilometre 'periji' (kaksha main dharti kaa sabase kareebi bindu) or 35,929 kilometre 'apoji' (kaksha main dharti kaa sabase dur bindu) ke 'jiosincronas transfar orbit' main bhej diya gaya
 From 31 August to 4 September, the Indian Space Research Organization (ISRO) will undertake three missions to lift the satellite into orbit to bring it to 'geostationary Orbit' 36,000 km above the equator

, President of Assocham

 arabiai ne repo dar or nakad aarakshi anupaat (siaraar) main 25 aadhaar ankon kii katautee kii he, jisase banking pranali main 18 hajaar karod rupee kii atirikt taralata kaa sanchaar hoga
 Fresh repo rate 7 after this deduction occurred after a long wait
 75 fisadi ho gai
 Earlier, in April 2012, the RBI had cut the repo and reverse repo rate by 50 basis points
 repo dar vah dar hoti he, jis par arabiai vanijyik bainkon ko choti avadhi ke karj detaa he
 Along with reduction in repo rate, reverse repo rate also reduced to 6
 75 fisadi ho gai
 The reverse repo rate is the rate at which RBI borrows from commercial banks for a short period
 is kadam se vanijyik bainkon ke liye karj lenaa sasta ho jayega or yadi is laabh ko graahakon tak bhi pahunchaaya gaya, to awaas, vaahan tathaa anya rinon par lagane vaali byaaj daren sasti ho sakati hai
 However, banks will take a decision on this issue on Wednesday
 arabiai ne siaraar ko bhi 25 aadhaar ank ghataakar 4
 00 per cent
 yah bainkon kii kul jamaa kaa vah anupaat hota he, jo unhen arabiai ke paas rakhana hota he
 This reduction in CRR will create additional liquidity of Rs 18 thousand crore in the market
 maudrik niti samiksha kii ghoshnaa main arabiai ke governor di
 Subbarao said, “this reduction in the cash reserve ratio will infuse primary liquidity of Rs 18 thousand crore in the banking system
 " RBI has cut key rates in line with market expectations
 thok keemton par aadhaarit desh kii mahangaai dar disambar main teen saalon ke nichle str par 7
 18 percent was recorded
 arabiai pehle hi jataa diya tha ki janvari-march timahi main daron main katautee ho sakati he, kyonki mahangaai ghatane ke asaar hai
 Union Commerce and Industry Minister Anand Sharma on Tuesday described the rbi's move as balanced and said rate cuts will increase liquidity and accelerate economic growth
 arabiai ke is kadam kaa udyog jagat ne tah-e-dil se swaagat kiya he
 Chandrajit Banerjee, director general of the Confederation of Indian Industry, said in a statement, "the government has started taking necessary steps to get the development process back on track
 udyog jagat ko khushi he ki arabiai ne yah bhi sanket diya he ki vah aage vikaas ko patari par laane ke liye sarkaar ke saath talmail bithayega
 " udyog jagat ke ek sanghathan fikki kii adhyaksh naina laal kidawai ne kaha, "haal hi main fikki ke aarthik paridrishy surveykshan main pratibhaagiyon ne aarthik vikaas main teji laane ke liye avilamb repo dar main 25 aadhaar ankon kii katautee or kaarobaari saal 2014 tak isamen 75 se 100 aadhaar ankon kii katautee kii vakaalat kii thi
 " asocham ke adhyaksh rajkumaar en
 Dhoot said, "reduction in both CRR and repo rate is a step in the right direction
 lekin bazaar ko ise sachhee bhaavana ke saath lenaa chahie or iskaa laabh aam logon ko bhi dena chahie
 " subbarao ne kaha ki samiksha main teen mukhya muddon par dhyaan diya gaya-mahangaai main narmi aane ke saath vikaas ko aage badhaane ke liye upyukt byaaj dar vyavastha bananaa, mahangaai ko rokna or utpaadak gatividhiyon ko karj dene ke liye pranali main samuchit taralata sunishchit karnaa
 The RBI also revised some estimates about the economy
 subbarao ne kaha ki maujuuda kaarobaari saal ke liye vikaas dar kaa anumaan 5
 5 per cent is placed, the first 5
 8 fisadi rakhaa gaya tha
 He said that the estimate of inflation by the end of March is 6

 Repo rate is the rate at which RBI gives short-term loans to commercial banks
 repo dar main katautee ke saath hi reverse repo rate bhi ghat kar 6
 75 percent
 reverse repo dar vah dar hoti he, jis par arabiai vanijyik bainkon se choti avadhi ke liye udhari letaa he
 The move will make it cheaper for commercial banks to take loans and if this benefit is passed on to customers, the interest rates on housing, vehicles and other loans may become cheaper
 haalanki bank is mudde par buudhvaar ko koi nirnay lenge
 RBI also reduced the CRR by 25 basis points to 4
 00 fisadi kar diya he
 It is the ratio of banks' total deposits that they have to keep with the RBI
 siaraar main is katautee se bazaar main 18 hajaar karod rupee kii atirikt taralata paidaa hogi
 RBI Governor D
 in announcing the Monetary Policy Review
 subbarao ne kaha, "nakad aarakshi anupaat main is katautee se banking pranali main 18 hajaar karod rupee kii praathmik taralata kaa sanchaar hoga
 " arabiai ne bazaar kii ummiido ke anuroop hi mukhya daron main katautee kii he
 The country's inflation based on wholesale prices is at a three-year low in December
 18 fisadi darj kii gai
 RBI had already expressed that the rates could be cut in the january-march quarter as inflation is expected to come down
 kendriya vaanijya or udyog mantri anand sharma ne mangalvaar ko arabiai ke kadam ko santulit bataaya or kaha ki dar katautee se taralata badhegi or aarthik vikaas main teji aegi
 This step of RBI has been welcomed by the industry with teh-e-dil
 bhartiya udyog parisangh ke mahanideshak chandrajit banerjee ne ek bayaan main kaha, "sarkaar ne vikaas kii prakriya ko waapas patari par laane ke liye jaruri kadam uthaane shuru kar die hai
 The industry is happy that the RBI has also indicated that it will coordinate with the government to bring development back on track
 " Naina Lal Kidwai, chairwoman of FICCI, an industry body, said, "recently, participants in ficci's Economic Scenario Survey cut the repo rate by 25 basis points to accelerate economic growth and from 75 to this by FY14 a reduction of 100 basis points was advocated
 " Rajkumar N
, President of Assocham
 dhoot ne kaha, "siaraar or repo dar donon hi main katautee sahi disha main uthaaya gaya kadam he
 But the market should take it with true spirit and give its benefits to the common people as well
 " Subbarao said that the review focused on three main issues - creating suitable interest rate regime to drive growth with inflation moderating, curbing inflation and ensuring proper liquidity in the system for lending to productive activities
 arabiai ne arthvyavastha ke bare main kuch anumaanon main sanshodhan bhi kiye
 Subbarao said that the growth rate for the current business year is estimated at 5
 5 fisadi rakhaa gaya he, jo pehle 5
 8 per cent was retained
 unhone kaha ki march ke ant tak mahangaai dar kaa anumaan 6
 8 per cent is placed, the first 7
 5 fisadi rakhaa gaya tha
 The announcement of a 25 basis point reduction in the repo rate and CRR by the RBI brought an immediate surge in the stock markets, but this boom did not last long

 somvaar ko maan-manouvval ke lambey daur ke baad bhi adwani nahin maane
 Now the voices of protest are intensifying in the party
 isaki shuruyaat adwani kheme ke netaaon ne kii he
 The first glimpse of the rebellion in the BJP was seen in the party's parliamentary board meeting on Monday night
 sutron ke mutabik is baithak main sushamaa swaraj, anant kumaar or venkaiya naidu ne adwani kii gairmaujuudagi main modi kii tajposhi par naaraazgi jataai
 These leaders said that there was no need for the party to show such haste over the coronation of Modi
 sutron kii maane to baithak main sushamaa, anant kumaar or venkaiya naidu ne anya netaaon ko aade haathon liya
 He said that due to the coronation of Modi, today the party is lying in this dispute
 modi ko lekar kiye gaye nirnay main bevajaah hadabadi dikhaai gai
 It is worth noting that even during the BJP executive meeting in Goa on 8-9 June, these leaders had raised questions about giving command to Modi in Advani's absence
 in netaaon kaa kahana tha ki adwani kii maujuudagi main hi modi ko chunaav prachaar samiti kaa chairman banaaya jaae to behatar hoga
 Voices of protest were also heard on Tuesday
 adwani samarthak maane jane vaale jaswant singh ne kaha ki adwani ne jo baaten kahi wo sahi hai or in sawaalon kaa samaadhaan hona chahie
 The question is, for what reason is Advani angry? Modi's coronation, or by the intervention of the RSS in bjp's work
 yaa phir donon
 If sources are to be believed, the main reason for Advani's displeasure is the attitude of the RSS and Modi's coronation was done by putting ghee in the fire
 is bich, adwani ko manaane kii kavayad lagaataar duusare din bhi jari he
 On Tuesday, Nitin Gadkari, Murali Manohar Joshi, Uma Bharti and Gopinath Munde met Advani
 vahiin, bijepi pravaktaa prakaash jaavdekar ne ummid jataai ki party is masale par samaadhaan nikaal legi or jald hi khushkhabari milegi
 Amid attempts to persuade Advani, party president Rajnath Singh has gone to Banswara in Rajasthan to unveil the statue of Maharana Pratap
 ravaanaa hone se pehle unhone adwani maamle main aresas se judi aa rahi khabaron ko bebuniyaad bataaya
 However, he did not say anything on persuading Advani
 gauratlab he ki somvaar raat ko aisi khabaren ain ki aresas ne party ko nirdesh diya he ki adwani ko manaane kii har koshish kii jaae par modi par liya faisla waapas nahin hoga
 bjp's problem is not ending here
 vipakshi bhi is puure vivaad par chutki lene kaa mauka nahin chook rahe
 Opponents even pasted Advani's resignation letter in the form of an overnight poster in the Lutyens zone, considered Delhi's VVIP
 haalanki ye harakat kisne kii he abhi iskaa pataa nahin chal sakaa he
 Above this poster is written, 'look Bha
 ja
 Pa
 kaa pardaafash'
 Posters have subsequently printed the same lines of Advani's letter in which he has accused BJP leaders of working for personal interests
 bharat or pakistan ke adhikariyon ne shuukravaar ko sauhardpurn maahaul main sikh tirthayatriyon ke liye prastaavit kartarpur galiyare kii sadakon or pul ke str jaise takneekee pahulon par charchaa main kii
 This is the first such meeting after increasing tension between the two countries over the abolition of special status of Jammu and Kashmir by India
 baithak main shaamil bhartiya rashtriya rajmarg praadhikaran (enechaeai) ke ek adhikari ne bataaya ki yah baithak ‘jiro point' par hui
 Explain that 'zero Point' is the point where the Indian part of the corridor and the Pakistani part will meet
 is baithak main prayek paksh ke 10 se 15 adhikariyon ne hissaa liya
 NHAI Chief Engineer TS Chahal said the meeting lasted for about two hours in which various technical aspects related to the corridor were discussed
 pakistan videsh mantralay ke ek adhikari se lahore main kaha ki yah sakaaratmak baithak thi or galiyara pariyojna ko samay par khatm karne ke sambandh main acchhee pragati hui
 The official said that the two sides also agreed to hold another meeting of technical experts to review the progress of the project
 pakistani adhikari ne kaha ki pariyojna ke raajnneetik pahulon par ek baithak bhi jald hi hogi
 He said that a memorandum of understanding (mou) will also be signed between the two countries on the corridor project in that meeting
 bharat kii taraf se baithak main grih mantralay, seemaa suraksha bal va bhartiya bhoomi pattan praadhikaran ke adhikariyon ne bhaag liya
 This authority is constructing the state-of-the-art passenger terminal building
 yah galiyara pakistan ke kartarpur main sthit darbar sahib ko gurdaspur jile ke deraa baba nanak gurudware se jodega or bhartiya sikh tirthayatriyon ko vija mukt awajahi kii suvidha pradaan karegaa
 Sikh pilgrims only need permission to visit Kartarpur Sahib
 guru nanak dev ne 1522 main kartarpur sahib kii sthapana kii thi
 India had repealed most of the provisions of Article 370 of the Constitution granting special status to Jammu and Kashmir on August 5 and divided the state into two union territories
 iske baad donon deshon ke bich yah pehali baithak he
 Chahal said technical issues such as proposed corridor roads and bridge levels were also discussed
 yatra ke dauraan tirthayatriyon ko pradaan kii jane vaali chikitsa suvidhaon par bhi charchaa kii gayi
 At the meeting held in temporary tents, the two sides discussed roads and other engineering aspects along with the completion time of the bridge
 chahal ne kaha ki baithak sauhardpurn maahaul main hui
 He said that various works related to the corridor would be completed just before the 550th birth anniversary of Guru Nanak Dev in November
 pakistan ke videsh mantralay ne donon deshon ke takneekee visheshgyon kii baithak ke bare main shuukravaar shaam tak koi bayaan jari nahin kiya tha kyonki vah ise zyada prachaarit-prasaarit nahin karnaa chahta tha
 On the appeal of Prime Minister Imran Khan, Pakistan chose Friday as the day to show solidarity with the Kashmiris
 baithak sthal par kadi suraksha vyavastha kii gai thi or parisar ke nikat kisi bhi media karmi ko jane kii anumati nahin thi
 Pakistan and India are considering modalities regarding the opening of the corridor at Narowal, about 125 km from Lahore, on November 12 to mark the 550th birth anniversary of Guru Nanak Dev
 kartarpur galiyare ko lekar pichley kuch maheenon main kai daur kii baithken hui hai jinamein donon pakshon ke visheshgyon ne vibhinn takneekee pahaluon par bhi baat kii he
 The delegations of the two countries held a meeting on the attari-wagah border towards Pakistan in July to discuss the modalities of the Kartarpur corridor
 yah galiyara 1947 ke baad se donon padosi deshon ke bich pehla vija mukt galiyara bhi hoga
 Pakistan is constructing the corridor from the Indian border to the Gurdwara Darbar Sahib while India will construct the second part from Dera Baba Nanak to the border
 uttarakhand ke mukhyamantri harish ravat ne ravivaar ko kaha ki vidhansabha chunaav ke liye 16 janvari tak congress pratyaashiyon kii suchi jari kar di jaaegi
 He told a press conference in Dehradun that till now out of the total 70 seats, 63 names have been agreed and the names of candidates will be decided soon on the remaining seven seats
 pradesh main 70-sadasyeey vidhansabha ke liye 15 farvari ko matdaan hoga
 Rawat's statement came after reports of differences between the chief minister and state Congress president Kishore Upadhyay over ticket distribution
 yah puche jane par ki kya unke tathaa pradesh adhyaksh ke bich tikaton ko lekar matbhed he? mukhyamantri ne isse inkaar karte hue kaha ki aisa nahin he
 He said, 'by January 16, the list of candidates of our party will be released
 ' On the other hand, Upadhyay also confirmed in a similar statement that the names of the candidates in 63 of the 70 seats have been agreed upon and the final list will be released after the Central Election Committee meeting is approved
